Greeting,<br>
<br>
FYI, we noticed the following commit (built with gcc-9):<br>
<br>
commit: 87b1c39af431a20ab69bdceb9036360cf58a28e4 ("[RFC PATCH 23/37] mm: rcu safe vma->vm_file freeing")<br>
url: <a  rel="nofollow" href="https://github.com/0day-ci/linux/commits/Michel-Lespinasse/Speculative-page-faults/20210407-095517">https://github.com/0day-ci/linux/commits/Michel-Lespinasse/Speculative-page-faults/20210407-095517</a><br>
base: <a  rel="nofollow" href="https://git.kernel.org/cgit/linux/kernel/git/tip/tip.git">https://git.kernel.org/cgit/linux/kernel/git/tip/tip.git</a> a500fc918f7b8dc3dff2e6c74f3e73e856c18248<br>
<br>
in testcase: nvml<br>
version: nvml-x86_64-09f75f696-1_20210402<br>
with following parameters:<br>
<br>
	test: pmem<br>
	group: blk<br>
	nr_pmem: 1<br>
	fs: ext4<br>
	mount_option: dax<br>
	bp_memmap: 32G!4G<br>
	ucode: 0x7000019<br>
<br>
<br>
<br>
on test machine: 16 threads Intel(R) Xeon(R) CPU D-1541 @ 2.10GHz with 48G memory<br>

	[ -n "$LKP_SRC" ] ||<br>
	export LKP_SRC=/lkp/${user:-lkp}/src<br>

<br>
run_job()<br>
{<br>
	echo $$ > $TMP/run-job.pid<br>
<br>
	. $LKP_SRC/lib/http.sh<br>
	. $LKP_SRC/lib/job.sh<br>
	. $LKP_SRC/lib/env.sh<br>
<br>
	export_top_env<br>
<br>
	run_setup nr_pmem=1 $LKP_SRC/setup/disk<br>
<br>
	run_setup fs='ext4' $LKP_SRC/setup/fs<br>
<br>
	run_setup bp_memmap='32G!4G' $LKP_SRC/setup/boot_params<br>
<br>
	run_monitor $LKP_SRC/monitors/wrapper kmsg<br>
	run_monitor $LKP_SRC/monitors/wrapper heartbeat<br>
	run_monitor $LKP_SRC/monitors/wrapper meminfo<br>
	run_monitor $LKP_SRC/monitors/wrapper oom-killer<br>
	run_monitor $LKP_SRC/monitors/plain/watchdog<br>
<br>
	run_test $LKP_SRC/tests/wrapper nvml<br>
}<br>
<br>
extract_stats()<br>
{<br>
	export stats_part_begin=<br>
	export stats_part_end=<br>
<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper nvml<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper kmsg<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper meminfo<br>
<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper time nvml.time<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper dmesg<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper kmsg<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper last_state<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper stderr<br>
	$LKP_SRC/stats/wrapper time<br>
}<br>
<br>
"$@"<br>
